      <wsdl:input wsaw:Action="http://www.superoffice.net/ws/crm/NetServer/Services84/Quote/GetQuoteAlternative" name="GetQuoteAlternativeRequest" message="tns:GetQuoteAlternativeRequest" />
      <wsdl:output wsaw:Action="http://www.superoffice.net/ws/crm/NetServer/Services84/Quote/GetQuoteAlternativeResponse" name="GetQuoteAlternativeResponse" message="tns:GetQuoteAlternativeResponse" />
    </wsdl:operation>
    <wsdl:operation name="RecalculateQuoteAlternative">
      <wsdl:documentation>
        <summary>When the user changes one or more values in a quoteline or a quoteAlternative, the connector gets to change the QuoteLines and the alternative, for instance calculate VAT. RecalculateQuoteAlternative shall be called when the user changes any of the following fields: Quantity, DiscountAmount, DiscountPercent, listprice (if allowed). RecalculateQuoteAlternative will calculate the TotalPrice and the VAT (if possible) for the lines and the alternative.</summary>
      </wsdl:documentation>
      <wsdl:input wsaw:Action="http://www.superoffice.net/ws/crm/NetServer/Services84/Quote/RecalculateQuoteAlternative" name="RecalculateQuoteAlternativeRequest" message="tns:RecalculateQuoteAlternativeRequest" />
      <wsdl:output wsaw:Action="http://www.superoffice.net/ws/crm/NetServer/Services84/Quote/RecalculateQuoteAlternativeResponse" name="RecalculateQuoteAlternativeResponse" message="tns:RecalculateQuoteAlternativeResponse" />
